<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a> (1666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратить.html>обрати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obraščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратить.html>обрати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn; to direct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо/что́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obraščátʹ</b> vnimánije na kovó-libo/štó-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to pay attention to someone/something</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо/что́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obraščátʹ</b> čʹjó-libo vnimánije na kovó-libo/štó-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to call / draw smb.'s attention to someone/something</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn into
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прах.html>прах</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obraščátʹ</b> v prax</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to reduce to dust / ashes</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to convert
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> католи́чество</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obraščátʹ</b> v katolíčestvo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to catholicize</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращаться.html>обращаться</a> (1159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obraščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращаться.html>обраща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obraščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратиться.html>обрати́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn to, to turn into</li>
<li>to address, to apply, to appeal</li>
<li>to advert <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to treat, to handle, to manage</li>
<li>to circulate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obraščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obraščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратить.html>обрати́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ние</a> (3050)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратить.html>обрати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращать.html>обраща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obraščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Common Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">обратити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obratiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obraščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conversion, transformation</li>
<li>circulation</li>
<li>treatment, management, handling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> manners</li>
<li>address, salutation</li>
<li>appeal</li></ol>

***обрез.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>обрез</a> (11085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obrézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>обре́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obréz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрез.html>обре́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрез.html>обре́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрез.html>обре́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>edge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of book pages, a roof, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>обре́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v obréz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">only just enough; very short</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>обре́з</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá vrémeni v <b>obréz</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have just enough time. / I have no time to spare.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sawn-off rifle, sawn-off shotgun</li></ol>

***обрезание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ние</a> (26140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obrézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обреза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obrezátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ние</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обре́зание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrezánije</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrézanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ния</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обре́зания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ния</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обре́зания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ний</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обре́заний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ние</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cutting, paring, trimming, edging</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обре́зание</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:обрезание.html>обреза́ние</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> circumcision</li></ol>

***обрезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обреза́ть</a> (12423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обре́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обреза́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обре́зывать</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cut off, to clip, to pare, to trim, to prune, to square
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обре́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>но́гти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obrézatʹ</b> nógti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pare one's fingernails</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрезать.html>обре́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obrézatʹ</b> pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut one's finger</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to circumcise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snub, to cut short</li></ol>

<ol><li>to cut off, to clip, to pare, to trim, to prune, to square

<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бре́мен-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brémen-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бремени́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bremenítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obrěsti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gain, to acquire, to be blessed with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obrestí</b> pokój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to find peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верный.html>ве́рных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obrestí</b> vérnyx druzéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to find faithful friends</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обрет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obret-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obretátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gain, to acquire, to be blessed with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obretátʹ</b> pokój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to find peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верный.html>ве́рных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obretátʹ</b> vérnyx druzéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to find faithful friends</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***обретаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обретаться.html>обрета́ться</a> (20045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obretátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретаться.html>обрета́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obretátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to abide, to pass one's time</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретать.html>обрета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obretátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obrestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обретение.html>обрете́ние</a> (19544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обрет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obret-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретение.html>обрете́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obreténije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретение.html>обрете́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретение.html>обрете́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обретение.html>обрете́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>acquisition; appropriation; discovery, finding</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрисовавший.html>обрисова́вший</a> (17903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрисовавший.html>обрисова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrisovávšij</span>)

***обрубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрубить.html>обруби́ть</a> (18060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>руби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрубить.html>обруби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obrubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обруба́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to trim by cutting off a part</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chop off, to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрубить.html>обруби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сук.html>сук</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рева</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obrubítʹ</b> suk s déreva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>cut off</b> a branch from the tree</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́дом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обрубить.html>обруби́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snarjádom <b>obrubílo</b> jevó rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a shell/projectile <b>cut off</b> his hand</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut off, to cut short, to interrupt abruptly (a person, one's sleep, etc.)</li>
<li>to hem</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обру́б</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obrúb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
